Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">C# Interview Questions and Answers - Part 11<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a></h3>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q101 What is Data Annotation in C#? How can you do remote validation
using it?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Data Annotations are Model Binder that is used to perform model
validation within a .NET application. The advantage of using the Data
Annotation validators is that they enable you to perform validation simply by
adding one or more attributes to a class property.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Data Annotations Model Binder is not an official part of the Microsoft
ASP.NET MVC framework. However the Data Annotations Model Binder was created by
the Microsoft ASP.NET MVC team, Microsoft does not offer official product
support for the Data Annotations Model Binder.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">For using the Data Annotations Model Binder in an ASP.NET MVC
application, you first need to add a reference to the
Microsoft.Web.Mvc.DataAnnotations.dll assembly and the
System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.dll assembly.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">The System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations namespace has a group of
classes, attributes, and methods, to make validations in our .NET applications
which include the following validator attributes:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Required:&nbsp;</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enables you to mark a property as required.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">StringLength:&nbsp;</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enables you to specify a maximum length for a string property.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">MaxLength:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enables you to specify the number of maximum and minimum elements
in the Array property.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">4.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Range:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enables you to validate whether the value of a property falls
between a specified range of values.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">5.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">RegularExpression:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enables you to validate whether the value of a property matches a
specified regular expression pattern.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">6.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Compare:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enable you to compare the value of two properties<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">7.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">DataType:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enable you to specify a type to any property like Email,
PhoneNumber, Password, CreditCard, PostalCode, Html, Currency, Url, DateTime,
etc.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">8.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Remote:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Enable you to do remote validation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">9.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">All the above attributes inherit the abstract class
ValidationAttribute. ValidationAttribute validates only one Property in the
object. It has an important property ErrorMessage which is used to get or set
the custom validation message in case of error.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">Model Validation in Entity Framework:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Since nowadays we are mostly using the Entity Framework. But if you
are using the Microsoft Entity Framework to generate your data model classes
then you cannot apply the validator attributes directly to your classes.
Because the Entity Framework Designer generates the model classes, any changes
you make to the model classes will be overwritten the next time you make any
changes in the Designer.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">If you want to use the validators with the classes generated by the
Entity Framework then you need to create metadata classes. You apply the
validators to the metadata class instead of applying the validators to the
actual class. For creating a metadata class you must have to use partial class
and methods. So please read the Partial Class article here and the Partial
Method article here for more details.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">Remote Validation:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> The Remote Attribute
is used for remote validation. For example to check instantly whether a record

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q102. What is Reflection? What is the use of reflection in C#?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><i><span lang="EN-US">In .Net Reflection allows you to fetch the <b>metadata information</b>
of a Type (Assembly) at runtime or programmatically. With reflection, we can
dynamically create an instance of a type, bind the type to an existing object,
or get the type from an existing object and invoke its methods or access its
fields and properties.&nbsp;</span></i><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">In .Net, during the compile-time Metadata is created with <b>MSIL</b>
and stored in a file called a <b>Manifest</b>. Both Metadata and Microsoft
Intermediate Language together wrapped in a <b>Portable Executable (PE) file</b>
and this can be accessed at runtime by a mechanism, called Reflection.<br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">At runtime, the Reflection mechanism uses the Portable Executable
file to read information about the assembly and it is possible to uncover the
methods, properties, and events of a type, and to invoke them
dynamically.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">The&nbsp;System.Reflection&nbsp;namespace
and&nbsp;System.Type&nbsp;class plays a vital role in .NET Reflection. These
two work together and allow you to reflect on many other aspects of a type.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">GetType() Method:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br>
The GetType() is a member of the System.Object class and the method return an
instance of <b>System.Type</b>. Reflection generally begins with a call to a
method present on every object in the .NET framework i.e GetType().&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">The main class for reflection is the <b>System.Type</b> class, which
is an abstract class representing a type in the <b>Common Type System</b>
(CTS).&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">The Type class and its members are used to get information about a
type declaration and its members such as class types, interface types, array
types, value types, enumeration types, type parameters, generic type
definitions, and open or closed constructed generic types, constructors,
methods, fields, properties, and events of a class.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">There are three way to get the type of any object i.e
System.Object.GetType(), System.Type.GetType() and <b>typeof ()</b> C#
operator.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">System.Reflection Namespace:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">The System.Reflection namespace contains classes and interfaces that
provide a managed view of loaded types, methods, and fields, with the ability
to dynamically create and invoke types; this process is known as Reflection in
the .NET framework.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">The classes in the <b>System.Reflection</b> namespace, together with
<b>System.Type</b>, enable you to obtain information about loaded assemblies
and the types defined within them, such as classes, interfaces, and value types
(that is, structures and enumerations). You can also use reflection to create
type instances at run time and to invoke and access them.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Reflection provides objects that encapsulate assemblies, modules,
and types. You can use reflection to dynamically create an instance of a type,
bind the type to an existing object, or get the type from an existing object.
You can then invoke the type's methods or access its fields and
properties.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br>
Reflection allows us to:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">1. <b>Use ConstructorInfo:</b> To discover information such as the
name, parameters, access modifiers (such as public or private), and
implementation details (such as abstract or virtual) of a constructor. Use the
GetConstructors or GetConstructor method of a Type to invoke a specific
constructor.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">2. <b>Use MethodInfo:</b>&nbsp; To discover information such as the
name, return type, parameters, access modifiers (such as public or private),
and implementation details (such as abstract or virtual) of a method. Use the
GetMethods or GetMethod method of a Type to invoke a specific method.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">3. <b>Use FieldInfo:</b>&nbsp; To discover information such as the
name, access modifiers (such as public or private), and implementation details
(such as static) of a field, and to get or set field values.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">4. <b>Use ParameterInfo:</b>&nbsp; To discover information such as a
parameter's name, data type, whether a parameter is an input or output
parameter, and the position of the parameter in a method signature.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">5. <b>Use PropertyInfo:</b>&nbsp; To discover information such as
the name, data type, declaring type, reflected type, and read-only or writable
status of a property, and to get or set property values.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">6. <b>Use Module:</b> To discover information such as the assembly
that contains the module and the classes in the module. You can also get all
global methods or other specific, non-global methods defined on the module.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">7. <b>Use Assembly:</b>&nbsp; To define and load assemblies, load
modules that are listed in the assembly manifest, locate a type from this
assembly and create an instance of it.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">•<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">Compilers for languages such as
JScript use reflection to construct symbol tables.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">•<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The classes in the
System.Runtime.Serialization namespace use reflection to access data and to
determine which fields to persist.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">•<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The classes in the <b>System.Runtime.Remoting</b>
namespace use reflection indirectly through serialization.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:

</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">Late bindings can also be
achieved through reflection.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q103. What is LINQ in C#?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ stands for Language
Integrated Query which provides a uniform query syntax in C# and VB.NET to
retrieve data from different sources and formats.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ is a data querying
methodology that provides querying capabilities to .NET languages with a syntax
similar to a SQL query.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ has great power of
querying on any source of data. The data source could be collections of
objects, databases or XML files.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">4.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ was introduced in .NET
Framework 3.5 to query the data from different sources of data.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">5.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The System.LINQ namespace
contains set of extension methods that allows us to query the source of data
object directly in our code based on the requirement.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">6.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">We can easily retrieve data
from any object that implements the IEnumerable&lt;T&gt; interface.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">7.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;LINQ queries return
results as objects. It enables you to use an object-oriented approach on the
result set and not to worry about transforming different formats of results
into objects. You will not get the result of a LINQ query until you execute it.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo3"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">8.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">At compile time, LINQ query
expressions are converted to Standard Query Operator method calls according to
the rules set forth in the C# specification.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="FirstParagraph"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">There are the following LINQ Objects available in the .Net:<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ to XML<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ To Entities<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">Advantages of LINQ:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ offers a common syntax for
querying any type of data source. LINQ offers an object-based,
language-integrated way to query over data no matter where that data came from.
So through LINQ, we can query databases, XML as well as collections.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">So LINQ bridges the gap and
strengthens the connection between relational data and the object-oriented
world<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ has Compile time syntax
checking. LINQ query expressions (unlike traditional SQL statements) are
strongly typed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">4.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">A LINQ query is not executed
until you iterate over the query variable, hence supporting deferred execution.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">5.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ offers IntelliSense which
means writing more accurate queries easily.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">6.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ offers the facility of
joining several data sources in a single query as well as breaking complex
problems into a set of short queries easy to debug.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo5"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">7.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">LINQ offers easy transformation
for conversion of one data type to another like transforming SQL data to XML
data.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
