<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q104. What is Extension Method in C#? What is the difference between
the Extension Method, Overloaded Method, and Overridden Method?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Extension methods enable you to "add" methods to existing
types without creating a new derived type, recompiling, or otherwise modifying
the original type. Extension methods are static methods, but they're called as
if they were instance methods on the extended type.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Extension methods are introduced in C# 3.0 with .NET 3.5. Extension
methods can be used as an approach to extending the functionality of a class in
the future if the source code of the class is not available or we don’t have
any permission in making changes to the class.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Before extension methods, inheritance is an approach that is used
for extending the functionality of a class i.e. if we want to add any new
members to an existing class without making a modification to the class, we
will define a child class to that existing class and then we add new members in
the child class.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">Components of an Extension Method:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Static Class:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> A static class contains all the extension methods.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Static Method:</span></b><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;A static method that defines the extension method.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo6"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span lang="EN-US">Binding Parameter:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> Type (class or interface) parameter with "this" keyword.
This will always be the first parameter decorated with "this" keyword
explicitly. Only one binding parameter is allowed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">You can use extension methods to extend a class or interface, but
not to override them. An extension method with the same name and signature as
an interface or class method will never be called. Extension methods can be
overloaded as well.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">At compile time, extension methods always have lower priority than
instance methods defined in the type itself. So if a type has a method named
Process(int i), and you have an extension method with the same signature, the
compiler will always bind to the instance method.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">When the compiler encounters a method invocation, it first looks for
a match in the type's instance methods. If no match is found, it will search
for any extension methods that are defined for the type, and bind to the first
extension method that it finds.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Please read more about method overloading </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.techpointfunda.com/2021/10/static-polymorphism-csharp.html"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:

main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q105. What are Anonymous Types in C#? How it is different from
dynamic types?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">In C#, an anonymous type is a type (class) without any name that can
contain public read-only properties only. Anonymous types provide a convenient
way to encapsulate a set of read-only properties into a single object without
having to explicitly define a type first. The type name is generated by the
compiler and is not available at the source code level. The type of each
property is inferred by the compiler.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Anonymous types typically are used in the select clause of a query
expression to return a subset of the properties from each object in the source
sequence. LINQ queries use the anonymous types most frequently.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Anonymous types contain one or more public read-only properties. No
other kinds of class members, such as methods or events, are valid. The expression
that is used to initialize a property cannot be null, an anonymous function, or
a pointer type.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Anonymous types are class types that derive directly from objects,
and that cannot be cast to any type except object.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">If two or more anonymous object initializers in an assembly specify
a sequence of properties that are in the same order and that have the same
names and types, the compiler treats the objects as instances of the same type.
They share the same compiler-generated type information.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">You cannot declare a field, a property, an event, or the return type
of a method as having an anonymous type. Similarly, you cannot declare a formal
parameter of a method, property, constructor, or indexer as having an anonymous
type.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">To pass an anonymous type or a collection that contains anonymous
types, as an argument to a method, you can declare the parameter as a type
object.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Typically, when you use an anonymous type to initialize a variable,
you declare the variable as an implicitly typed local variable by using var.
The type name cannot be specified in the variable declaration because only the
compiler has access to the underlying name of the anonymous type. You create
anonymous types by using the new operator together with an object initializer.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">C# 4</span></b><span lang="EN-US"> introduces a new type i.e.&nbsp;<b>dynamic</b>.
The type is a static type, but an object of type dynamic bypasses static type
checking.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">In most cases, it functions like it has a type object. At compile
time, an element that is typed as dynamic is assumed to support any operation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">We can convert a dynamic object to other types very easily. This
enables the developer to switch between dynamic and non-dynamic behavior.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Overload resolution occurs at run time instead of at compile time if
one or more of the arguments in a method call has the type dynamic, or if the
receiver of the method call is of type dynamic.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q106. What is the difference between dynamic and var type in C#?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">Var type is introduced in C#
3.0 while the dynamic type is introduced in C# 4.0.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">For var type the variable
initialization is mandatory but it is not mandatory in the case of dynamic.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">A var variable type is decided
by the right-hand side initializer but in the case of dynamic the compiler uses
Object type by default.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">4.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">A var type variable cannot be
initialized with a null value but a dynamic variable can be initialized with a
null value.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">5.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The variables declared using
the <b>var</b> keyword are statically typed while variables declared using the <b>dynamic</b>
keyword are dynamically typed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">6.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">For var, the type of the
variable is decided by the compiler at compile time. But in the case of dynamic
the type of the variable is decided by the compiler at run time.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">7.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">A var type supports <b>IntelliSense</b>
in the visual studio because they are known at compile time but a dynamic type
does not support any IntelliSense.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">8.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">A var type cannot be used for
properties or returning values from the function but a dynamic type can be used
for properties or returning values from the function.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo7"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">9.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">For a var type variable there
will be no </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://youtu.be/lruQ-1X4JWk"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">boxing and unboxing</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"> but in the case of dynamic type Boxing and Unboxing happen.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="FirstParagraph"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">

<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q107.&nbsp;&nbsp;What is the difference between the “throw” and
“throw ex” in .NET?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Sometimes we use a throw statement in the catch block to throw the
exception to log the exception. So there are two ways to throw the exception
throw and throw ex.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">If we use the "throw" statement i.e throw; it preserves
original error stack information. In exception handling "throw" with
an empty parameter is also called re-throwing the last exception.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">If we use the "throw ex" statement i.e throw(ex); the
stack trace of exception will be replaced with a stack trace starting at the
re-throw point. It is used to intentionally hide stack trace information.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">“throw” and “throw ex”:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo8"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">Both are used to throw
exceptions in the catch block to log messages.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo8"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">Both contain the same message
of the exception.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="FirstParagraph"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">“throw” vs “throw ex”:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo9"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">A throw is used to throw the
current exception while a throw(ex) is mostly used to create a wrapper of
exception.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo9"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The throw(ex) will reset your
stack trace so the error will appear from the line where throw(ex) is written
while the throw does not reset the <b>stack trace</b> and you will get
information about the original exception.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo9"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">In MSIL code when you use
throw(ex) it will generate code as throw and if you use the throw it will
create rethrow.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q108. What is finally block? How many finally blocks can you define
with a try block?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">A finally block is an optional block that comes after a try or
catches block.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Finally block is used to execute a given set of statements, whether
an exception is thrown or not thrown because a&nbsp; finally block will always
be executed whether an exception is raised or not. Hence it is generally used
to release unmanaged resources<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Only one finally block is allowed for a given try-catch block. But
it is possible to define a finally block without the catch block.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US">Q110. What is the difference between the IS and AS Operators in C#?<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><b><span lang="EN-US">IS Operator:</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo10"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">1.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The "IS" operator is
used to check whether the run-time type of an object is what we expect it to
be.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo10"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">2.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">It is a binary operator that
returns a Boolean indicating whether or not the instance is in fact of the type
specified as the second operand.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo10"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">3.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">In C# 6 and earlier, the IS
operator checks if the result of an expression are compatible with a given
type.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo10"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">4.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">But beginning with C# 7.0, you
can also use the IS operator to match an expression against a pattern.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo10"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">5.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">Beginning with C# 9.0, you can
use a negation pattern to do a non-null check.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="Compact" style="margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo10"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin"><span style="mso-list:Ignore">6.<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span lang="EN-US">The IS operator takes into
account boxing and unboxing conversions implicitly.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="FirstParagraph"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:

Xf455a7b1a80c64de5ef66f6cf64960e8b6213e4"><span style="mso-bookmark:outer-wrapper"><span lang="EN-US"><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br style="mso-special-character:line-break">
<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoBodyText"><span style="mso-bookmark:main"><span style="mso-bookmark:
main-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:content-wrapper"><span style="mso-bookmark:sunday-july-31-2022"><span style="mso-bookmark:Blog1"><span style="mso-bookmark:Xd0b102cc2bbe28657a1d393d44c8320f953898a"><span style="mso-bookmark:post-body-6432018817224884070"><span style="mso-bookmark:
